mirefleur full ſatisfaction ſhall bee made vnto ſorrowes anguiſhes haue ſuffered ouer feruent loue herewithall faire forlorne ſo greatly rauiſhed long time hee could anſwer one word hee tooke letter gaue great preſumption euery man imagine brunco ſhould obtaine victory ſo fell hee purſued madamain ſo neere brought extreamity almoſt breath ſayd vnto brunco doe beleeue conſidering rage thou art thou imagineſt day bee long enough end quarrell howbeit thou doeſt conſider thy armour almoſt vnriuited thou ſhalt finde better thee reſt thy ſelfe aſſaile mee ſo vndiſcreetly thou doeſt therefore vnwilling vſe thee ſo rigourouſly thou deſerueſt content giue thee leaue take breath may afterwards begin fight hotly brunco anſwered thou declareſt plaine tearmes needfull thy ſelfe wherefore pray thee luſtie thou art ſpare mee whit art thou ignorant occaſion combate knoweſt thou either thy head mine muſt ceaſe ſtrife doe aſſure thee determined liſten vnto thy preaching wherefore thou determine dy preſently looke thine owne defence better thou haſt done heretofore immediately without diſputations hee aſſailed madamain afreſh hee already ſo weake able ſo much defend brunco blowes hee drew himſelfe little little top rock euen place amadis caſt body ardan sea brunco thruſt ſo rudely downe ſent buried sea hee came bottome body torne twenty ſeuerall peeces iniurious damoſell perceiuing ſhe haue choſen graue raging sea beare companie ſo caſting herſelfe downe headlong ſhe immediately couered water brunco mounting horſebacke againe conducted king many knight lodging amadis hee deſired amadis commanded enil conduct deſire iſania gouernor thereof doe honour giue beſt entertainement hee could deuiſe briolania departed bidding oriana farewell aſſuring ſhe ſhould aduertiſed happened brocadan receiuing counſell good afterwards imprint king minde ſo great iealoſie ſurpition againſt amadis fellowes day hee hated ſo ſtrange ſort hee could manner abide ſee forgetting great ſeruices digreſſed bound reaſon although like malady doth often haunt al prince take heed falling like accident danger king liſuart giuing credit deceitfull word theſe traitor neuer afterwards viſit hee accuſtomed amadis others wounded whereat little abaſhed doe diſpite ſent madaſima pledge vnto ſayde within eight dayes iſle mongaza yeelded vnto according promiſe hee would ſuddainly cauſe head ſmitten madaſima heard rigorous conſtraint neuer woman afraid conſidering performing king ſhee ſhould remaine poore vtterly diſhereted ſide denying ſatisfie beheſt ſhee ſee death prepared ſo ſhe ſuch opinion therefore one day gandandel perſeuered aduertiſements amadis angry anſwered lord gandandel doe greatly wonder mooueth vſe ſpeech ſo often vnto ſeeing neuer thinke vpon thing onely wherein
